In [25]:
def CostFunction(X, y, m, b):
    errors = np.array([])
    
    for i in range(len(X)):
        prediction = m * X[i] + b
        observation = y[i]
        error = (observation - prediction) ** 2
        errors = np.append(errors, error)
    
    sum_errors = errors.sum()
    size = float(len(X))
    correction_factor = 1 / (2 * size)
    return correction_factor * sum_errors

def OneStep(X, y, m_current, b_current, learning_rate):
    size = float(len(X))
    
    m_gradient = 0
    for i in range(len(X)):
        m_gradient += (y[i] - (m_current * X[i] + b_current)) * (-X[i])
    m_gradient = (1 / size) * m_gradient
    print("m_current : ", m_current)
    print("m_gradient : ", m_gradient)
    
    b_gradient = 0
    for i in range(len(X)):
        b_gradient += (y[i] - (m_current * X[i] + b_current)) * (-1)
    b_gradient = (1 / size) * b_gradient
    print("b_current : ", b_current)
    print("b_gradient : ", b_gradient)
    
    m_new = m_current - learning_rate * m_gradient
    b_new = b_current - learning_rate * b_gradient
    
    print("learning_rate : ", learning_rate)
    print("m_new : ", m_new)
    print("b_new : ", b_new)
    
    return m_new, b_new
    
    
def LinearRegression(X, y, learning_rate, num_iterations):
    m = 0
    b = 0
    for i in range(num_iterations):
        m, b = OneStep(X, y, m, b, learning_rate)
    return m, b
